***прощать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a> (2449)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proščátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to forgive, to pardon, to excuse</li>
<li>to remit</li>
<li>to condone, to overlook</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">imperative  only</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to farewell</li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:извинять.html>извиня́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">izvinjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́ться</a> (3574)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:попрощаться.html>попроща́ться</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проститься.html>прости́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to say goodbye, to bid farewell
<ul><li><dl><dd><div class="wiktQuote" data-validation="white">Марко <a href = vnd.unilang:полый.html>По́ло</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:книга.html>Книга</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чудо.html>чуде́с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свет.html>све́та</a></i> :<dl><dd><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:когда.html>когда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:посол.html>посла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:уходить.html>уходи́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:домой.html>домо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:прощаться.html>проща́лись</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:царица.html>цари́ца</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:расставание.html>расстава́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горький.html>го́рько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плакать.html>пла́кала</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kogdá tri poslá uxodíli domój i <b>proščálisʹ</b>, tak caríca na rasstavánii górʹko plákala</i></dd><dd>when the three ambassadors parted home and <b>bade farewell</b> the queen bitterly wept at the valedictory</dd></dl></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощать.html>проща́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proščátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощальный.html>проща́льный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">proščálʹnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:прощение.html>проще́ние</a> (4361)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:простить.html>прости́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prostítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-énije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощение.html>проще́ние</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proščénije</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощение.html>проще́ния</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощение.html>проще́ния</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощение.html>проще́ний</a></b>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощупать.html>прощу́пать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">proščúpatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощупывать.html>прощу́пывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">proščúpyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прощупать.html>прощу́пать</a></b>)

***проявить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a> (2823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">про-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pro-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:явить.html>яви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">javítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projavítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show, to display, to evince, to manifest, to reveal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:забота.html>забо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projavítʹ</b> zabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show concern, to take trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projavítʹ</b> interés</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show interest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projavítʹ</b> sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show one's worth, to prove</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">photography</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to develop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">прояви́тель</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">projavítelʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">проявка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">projavka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>проя́вленный</a> (2823)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***проявлять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a> (3584)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projavítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-я́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-játʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projavljátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявить.html>прояви́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to show, to display, to evince, to manifest, to reveal
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:забота.html>забо́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projavljátʹ</b> zabótu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show concern, to take trouble</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:интерес.html>интере́с</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projavljátʹ</b> interés</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show interest</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:проявлять.html>проявля́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:себя.html>себя́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>projavljátʹ</b> sebjá</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to show one's worth, to prove</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(photograph)</i> to develop</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проявление.html>проявле́ние</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">projavlénije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прояснить.html>проясни́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projasnítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проясниться.html>проясни́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projasnítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проясняться.html>проясня́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clear <i>(become better seen)</i></li>
<li><i>(face)</i> to brighten <i>(up)</i></li>
<li><i>(weather)</i> to clear <i>(up)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>ве́черу</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проясниться.html>проясни́лось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k véčeru <b>projasnílosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the skies cleared towards the evening</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to clear <i>(up)</i>, to clarify, to become clearer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мысль.html>мы́слях</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проясниться.html>проясни́лось</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v mýsljax u nevó <b>projasnílosʹ</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">his mind cleared</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***прояснявшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проясняться.html>проясня́вшийся</a> (21210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***проясняться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:проясняться.html>проясня́ться</a> (21210)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прояснять.html>проясня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projasnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проясняться.html>проясня́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">projasnjátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проясниться.html>проясни́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to clear <i>(become better seen)</i></li>
<li><i>(face)</i> to brighten <i>(up)</i></li>
<li><i>(weather)</i> to clear <i>(up)</i></li>
<li>to clear <i>(up)</i>, to clarify, to become clearer
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ситуация.html>ситуа́ция</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:проясняться.html>проясня́ется</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">situácija <b>projasnjájetsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">the situation is clarifying; things are getting clearer now</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прояснять.html>проясня́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">projasnjátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***пруд.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>пруд</a> (4522)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">прудъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">prudŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stream, pressure, dam</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prǫdъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">prąd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flow, current</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovak_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovak language">Slovak</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sk">prúd</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">flow, current</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Slovene_language" class="extiw" title="w:Slovene language">Slovene</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sl">prod</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">gravel</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>пруд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">prud</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>пруда́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>пру́да</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>пруды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пруд.html>прудо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>pond</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:озерцо.html>озерцо́</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ozercó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*prǫžina</i>. ***пружинить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пружинить.html>пружи́нить</a> (16074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пружина.html>пружи́на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pružína</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пружинить.html>пружи́нить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pružínitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to be elastic, to be springy, to spring back, to yield</li>
<li>to tense (one's muscles)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:пружинящий.html>пружи́нящий</a> (16074)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пружинящий.html>пружи́нящий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">pružínjaščij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">present active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пружинить.html>пружи́нить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">pružínitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>
